***карандаш.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:карандаш.html>каранда́ш</a> (2681)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>In Russian from the 16–17th centuries. Borrowing from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> language. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">karataş</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">black slate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, composed of <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">kara</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">black</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">taş</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt"><a href = vnd.unilang:кара.html>ка́ра</a> таш</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qara taş</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">graphite, black lead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The origin of epenthetic <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-н-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-n-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is unclear. Perhaps it was added in colloquial Russian speech to ease the pronunciation. Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каланча.html>каланча́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kalančá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for the same epenthesis.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карандаш.html>каранда́ш</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">karandáš</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карандаш.html>карандаша́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карандаш.html>карандаши́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карандаш.html>карандаше́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pencil
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:карандаш.html>каранда́ш</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U tebjá jestʹ <b>karandáš</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Do you have <b>a pencil</b>?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***каратэ.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:каратэ.html>каратэ</a> (24955)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Japanese language">Japanese</a></span> <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">空手</i>, from <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">唐手</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-tr tr">karate</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Okinawan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Okinawan language">Okinawan</a></span> <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ryu">唐手</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ryu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tūdī</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">empty hand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каратэ.html>каратэ́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">karatɛ́</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>karate</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кардинал.html>кардина́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kardinál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кардинал.html>кардина́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кардинал.html>кардина́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кардинал.html>кардина́лов</a></b>)

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">carré</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">square</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кара.html>каре́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">karɛ́</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> square</li>
<li><i>(as an adjective)</i> square
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырез.html>вы́рез</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кара.html>каре</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:платье.html>пла́тья</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">výrez <b>kare</b> (u plátʹja)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">square cut</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(women's haircut)</i> bob
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кара.html>каре</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nosítʹ <b>kare</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wear one's hair in a bob</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кара.html>каре</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sdélatʹ sebé <b>kare</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">have one's hair bobbed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poker</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> four of a kind</li></ol>

***каркать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:каркать.html>ка́ркать</a> (16355)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каркать.html>ка́ркать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kárkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каркнуть.html>ка́ркнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to caw</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">deprecative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prophesy ill, to be a prophet of doom
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нака́ркать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nakárkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***каркнувший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:каркнувший.html>ка́ркнувший</a> (22981)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***карлик.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:карлик.html>ка́рлик</a> (7459)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">karel</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">karlík</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">karlę</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">karzeł</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">karlik</i>, all from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">karal</i>, whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">karl</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">little boy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kerl</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">young man</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карлик.html>ка́рлик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kárlik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карлик.html>ка́рлика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карлик.html>ка́рлики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карлик.html>ка́рликов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ка́рлица</b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карликовый.html>ка́рликовый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dwarf (<i>various senses</i>), midget, gnome, pygmy, manikin, elf</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Magic: The Gathering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a gnome</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карлик.html>ка́рлик</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kárlik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:карликовый.html>ка́рликовая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:планета.html>плане́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kárlikovaja</b> planéta</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>dwarf</b> planet</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карман.html>карма́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">karmán</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карман.html>карма́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карман.html>карма́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карман.html>карма́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pocket
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:карман.html>карма́не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:блоха.html>блоха́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:аркан.html>арка́не</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá v <b>karmáne</b> bloxá na arkáne!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’m flat broke!</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">I have a flea on a lasso in my <b>pocket</b>!</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карманник.html>карма́нник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">karmánnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карманник.html>карма́нника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карманник.html>карма́нники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карманник.html>карма́нников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">карма́нница</b>)
